                       <div data-reactid="1669">
                        <div data-reactid="1670">
                         Walker Cottage was originally a dog trot home, with additions became a one story farmhouse occupied by the Walker family for over 100 years. With our remodel, a lovely two story farmhouse we hope all our guests enjoy as our family does. 
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1671">
                         Walker Cottage is a 100+ year old farmhouse, lovingly restored to a three bedroom, 2-king, 1-double, and one and one-half bath, living room, den, fully equipped kitchen, washer/dryer, cable tv, upstairs sitting room and game room. Front porch for relaxing and watching Ashley Creek roll by. Homestead Entry in 1862, owned by W.C. and Minnie Walker, with the next four generations of Walker family living in the homeplace until 2003. Serene setting along Ashley Creek, cozily surrounded by tree covered ridges. Less than a mile to Ashley Creek landing on beautiful Blue Mountain Lake, twenty miles to the top of Mount Magazine State Park, and just minutes to the Arkansas Game &amp; Fish Field Trial Headquarters. Fishing, boating, swimming, hiking, horseback riding and ATV trails within minutes, or search for antiques and collectibles nearby, or in the farmhouse! Day trips from Walker Cottage, just a two hour drive to Fayetteville, Eureka Springs, Hot Springs or Little Rock. An hour west to Casinos just over the Arkansas-Oklahoma State line. Experience what the Walker family loved and enjoyed for over 140 years at Walker Cottage.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1672">
                         We enjoy the quiet country setting, listening to the creek and watching the deer come down from the ridge for their morning and evening visits.
                        </div>
